var subsFulfillmentFrequencyAttrName = "fulfillmentFrequency";
var subsPaymentFrequencyAttrName = "paymentFrequency";
var subsTimePeriodAttrName = "timePeriod";

//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
//Description: Dojo does not handle the case where the parameters in the URL are delimeted by the "/" forward slash. Therefore, in order to
//             workaround the issue, all AJAX requests must be done using absolute URLs rather than relative.
//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
function getAbsoluteURL()
{
	if (absoluteURL != "") {
		var currentURL = document.URL;
		var currentProtocol = "";
	
		if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
			currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
		
		var savedProtocol = "";
		if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
			savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
		
		if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
			absoluteURL = currentProtocol + absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
	}
	
	return absoluteURL;
}
//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the shared image directory.
//Description: In order to get the image directory path in any javascript file, this function can be used.
//Returns: The path to reference images.
function getImageDirectoryPath()
{
	return imageDirectoryPath;
}
//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the directory containing color-dependant image files.
//Description: In order to get the directory containing color-dependant image files in any javascript file, this function can be used.
//Returns: The path to reference color-dependant image files.
function getStyleDirectoryPath()
{
	return styleDirectoryPath;
}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   dojo.addOnLoad(function() {
	var nodes = dojo.query(".pr-snippet-read-write a.pr-snippet-link");
		if (nodes.length&gt;0){
			for (var i=0;i&lt;nodes.length;i++){ 
					if (nodes[i].innerHTML.toLowerCase()=="read review"){ 
						nodes[i].innerHTML = "read reviews";
					} 
					
					else if (nodes[i].innerHTML.toLowerCase()=="write a review"){ 
						nodes[i].innerHTML = "write review";
					}
			}
		}
	});
  </script>

       <script type="text/Javascript">
        function toggleActivityTable(tableId) {
			var arrowElement = document.getElementById("activityArrowId_" + tableId);
			var rowElement = document.getElementById("activityTableExpandId_" + tableId);
			if(arrowElement.className == "opened") {
				arrowElement.className = "unopened";
				rowElement.style.display = "none";
			}
			else {
				arrowElement.className = "opened";
				rowElement.style.display = "block";
			}
		}
       </script>

    <script>
     var LAT_SECURE_FITREC_JS_URL='https://lat-cdns.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/lat/js/fitrec.js';		
	var LAT_SECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL='https://lat-cdns.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/lat/js/jqModal.js';
	var LAT_NONSECURE_FITREC_JS_URL='http://lat-cdn.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/lat/js/fitrec.js';		
	var LAT_NONSECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL='http://lat-cdn.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/lat/js/jqModal.js';	
	var BAY_SECURE_FITREC_JS_URL='https://bay-cdns.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/bay/js/fitrec.js';	
	var BAY_SECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL='https://bay-cdns.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/bay/js/jqModal.js';
	var BAY_NONSECURE_FITREC_JS_URL='http://bay-cdn.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/bay/js/fitrec.js';
	var BAY_NONSECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL='http://bay-cdn.truefitcorp.com/fitrec/bay/js/jqModal.js';
	var TFDisplayStyle='BAY';
	
	function loadjscssfile(){
		var isSecured = false;
		if(location.href.indexOf("https://") !=-1){
		   isSecured = true;
		} 
		 if (isSecured){
			 if('LT'===TFDisplayStyle)  {
				  var fileref1=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref1.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref1.setAttribute("src", LAT_SECURE_FITREC_JS_URL);
		
				  var fileref2=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref2.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref2.setAttribute("src",LAT_SECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL);
			 }else if('BAY'===TFDisplayStyle){
				  var fileref1=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref1.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref1.setAttribute("src", BAY_SECURE_FITREC_JS_URL);
		
				  var fileref2=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref2.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref2.setAttribute("src", BAY_SECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL);
			 }
		} else{
			if('LT'===TFDisplayStyle)  {
				  var fileref1=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref1.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref1.setAttribute("src", LAT_NONSECURE_FITREC_JS_URL);
		
				  var fileref2=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref2.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref2.setAttribute("src",LAT_NONSECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL);
			 }else if('BAY'===TFDisplayStyle){
				  var fileref1=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref1.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref1.setAttribute("src", BAY_NONSECURE_FITREC_JS_URL);
		
				  var fileref2=document.createElement('script');
				  fileref2.setAttribute("type","text/javascript");
				  fileref2.setAttribute("src", BAY_SECURE_JQMODAL_JS_URL);
			 }
		}
		if (typeof fileref1!="undefined") document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(fileref1);
		if (typeof fileref2!="undefined") document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(fileref2);
	}
	loadjscssfile(); //dynamically load  .js file
    </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        dojo.addOnLoad(function(){

					if(dojo.byId('kleinfeldCategoryURL')!=null)
					{
						var kleinfeldHomepage=dojo.byId('kleinfeldCategoryURL').value;

							location.href=kleinfeldHomepage;

       </script>
       <script type="text/javascript">
        if(window.location.pathname.search("AjaxOrderItemDisplayView")&lt;0 &amp;&amp; window.location.pathname.search("OrderShippingBillingView")&lt;0){
						var shopbagdisplay = document.getElementById("outerCartContainer");
						shopbagdisplay.innerHTML='&lt;span id="bagItems" onmouseover="showMiniShopCartDropDown(\'placeHolder\',\'quick_bag\',\'orderItemsList\');"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div dojoType="wc.widget.RefreshArea" id="MiniShoppingCart" widgetId="MiniShoppingCart" controllerId="MiniShoppingCartController" role="wairole:region" waistate:live="polite" waistate:atomic="true" waistate:relevant="all"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
					}

					//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
					//Description: Dojo does not handle the case where the parameters in the URL are delimeted by the "/" forward slash. Therefore, in order to
					//	workaround the issue, all AJAX requests must be done using absolute URLs rather than relative.
					//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
					function getAbsoluteURL()
					{

						quickInfoPage = (('undefined' === typeof quickInfoPage) || (quickInfoPage === null)) ? false : quickInfoPage;

						if (('undefined' === typeof absoluteURL)) {
							var absoluteURL = "";
						}

						if (absoluteURL != "") {
							var currentURL = document.URL;
							var currentProtocol = "";

							if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
								currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL.indexOf("://"));
							}

							var savedProtocol = "";
							if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
								savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
							}

							if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
								absoluteURL = currentProtocol + absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
							}
						}

						return absoluteURL;
					}

					dojo.addOnLoad(function(){
						UtilitiesJS.displayBagItems();

						CommonContextsJS.setCommonParameters('-24','10701','10652');
						CommonControllersDeclarationJS.setCommonParameters('-24','10701','10652');
						CommonControllersDeclarationJS.setControllerURL('MiniShoppingCartController', getAbsoluteURL()+'AjaxQuickCartDisplay?storeId=10701&amp;catalogId=10652&amp;langId=-24');

						if(dojo.byId('MiniShoppingCart') != null){
							originalMiniCartWidth = dojo.coords(dojo.byId('MiniShoppingCart'),true).w;
						}
					});
       </script>

    <script type="text/Javascript">
     function toggleActivityTable(tableId) {
			var arrowElement = document.getElementById("activityArrowId_" + tableId);
			var rowElement = document.getElementById("activityTableExpandId_" + tableId);
			if(arrowElement.className == "opened") {
				arrowElement.className = "unopened";
				rowElement.style.display = "none";
			}
			else {
				arrowElement.className = "opened";
				rowElement.style.display = "block";
			}
		}
    </script>

						var parameters = {};
						  parameters.storeId = this.storeId;
						  parameters.langId=this.langId;
						  parameters.catalogId=this.catalogId;
						  parameters. evtype= "CpgnClick";

						    url: "ClickInfo",				
						    handleAs: "json-comment-filtered",
						    content: parameters,
						    service: this,
						    load:  ""
						  });
		window.location= destinationURL
}
